 Welcoming the proposed amendment, Senior Advocate of the Supreme Court PN Lekhi said that crimes like murder in the name of non-gratitude are social crimes and strict laws are needed to prevent them
 lekhi ne kaha ki bhartiya dand samhita main sanshodhan ke saath saath logon ko shikshit karnaa bhi jaruri he kyonki isaki rokthaam ke liye keval kanoon hi paryaapt nahin he

 baharhaal, kuch vidhi visheshgyon kii raay he ki alag kanoon banane kii koi jarurat nahin he or vartmaan kanoonon ko prabhavi tareeke se karyanvit karne par is samasya se nipta ja saktaa he
 Retired Judge of the Supreme Court Arun Kumar said that the change in the Indian Penal Code will not affect the current trend
 unhone kaha ki logon ko jaagruk bananaa or vartmaan kanoonon kaa prabhavi tathaa kadai se karyanvayan zyada jaruri he
